  19 #include <stdint.h>
  20 
  21 #include <jis0212.h>
  22 
  23 /* The defined JIS 0201 positions contains large gaps.  It's better to
  24    avoid using one large table with such big gaps.  Instead we match each
  25    char in a table resulting in an index to a table with the UCS.  The
  26    following command can be used to generate the table:
  27 
  28    egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
  29      .../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | perl tab.pl
  30 
  31    where tab.pl is
  32 
  33    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  34    $first=$last=$idx=0;
  35    while (<>) {
  36      local($jis,$ucs,%rest) = split;
  37      local($u)=hex($ucs);
  38      local($j)=hex($jis);
  39      local($k) = int(($j - 0x2121) / 256) * 94 + (($j - 0x2121) % 256);
  40      if ($k - $last > 6) {
  41        if ($last != 0) {
  42      printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d },\n",
  43          $first, $last, $idx);
  44      $idx += $last - $first + 1;
  45        }
  46        $first=$k;
  47      }
  48      $last=$k;
  49    }
  50    printf (" { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d }\n",
  51        $first, $last, $idx);
  52    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  53 */
  54 const struct jisx0212_idx __jisx0212_to_ucs_idx[] =
  55 {
  56  { .start = 0x006c, .end = 0x0076, .idx =     0 },
  57  { .start = 0x007f, .end = 0x0081, .idx =    11 },
  58  { .start = 0x00a8, .end = 0x00ae, .idx =    14 },
  59  { .start = 0x0216, .end = 0x0231, .idx =    21 },
  60  { .start = 0x0255, .end = 0x0261, .idx =    49 },
  61  { .start = 0x0285, .end = 0x0291, .idx =    62 },
  62  { .start = 0x02f0, .end = 0x02ff, .idx =    75 },
  63  { .start = 0x0310, .end = 0x031f, .idx =    91 },
  64  { .start = 0x034e, .end = 0x03a4, .idx =   107 },
  65  { .start = 0x03ac, .end = 0x0402, .idx =   194 },
  66  { .start = 0x0582, .end = 0x1c2a, .idx =   281 },
  67  { .start = 0xffff, .end = 0xffff, .idx =     0 },
  68 };
  69 
  70 
  71 /* The table which the UCS values indexed by the table above can be
  72    generated using the following code:
  73 
  74    egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
  75      .../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | perl tab.pl
  76 
  77    where tab.pl is:
  78 
  79    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
  80    $first=$last=$idx=0;
  81 
  82    sub fmt {
  83      printf ("\n ") if (($n % 8) == 0);
  84      ++$n;
  85      my($val) = pop(@_);
  86      printf (" %#06x,", $val);
  87    }
  88 
  89    while (<>) {
  90      local($jis,$ucs,%rest) = split;
  91      local($u)=hex($ucs);
  92      local($j)=hex($jis);
  93      local($k) = int(($j - 0x2121) / 256) * 94 + (($j - 0x2121) % 256);
  94      if ($k - $last > 6) {
  95        if ($last != 0) {
  96      $idx += $last - $first + 1;
  97        }
  98        $first=$k;
  99      } else {
 100        for ($m = $last + 1; $m < $k; ++$m) {
 101          fmt (0);
 102        }
 103      }
 104      fmt ($u);
 105      $last=$k;
 106    }
 107    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
 108 */

 873 
 874 
 875 /* The UCS char covered by JIS X0212 are sparsely distributed.  So we
 876    use again a two-step mapping table.  The index table can be computed
 877    using
 878 
 879    egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
 880      ../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | awk '{ print $2, $1 }' | sort -u |
 881    perl tab.pl
 882 
 883    where tab.pl is
 884 
 885    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
 886    $first=$last=$idx=0;
 887    while (<>) {
 888      local($ucs,$jis,%rest) = split;
 889      local($u)=hex($ucs);
 890      local($j)=hex($jis);
 891      if ($u - $last > 6) {
 892        if ($last != 0) {
 893      printf ("  { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d },\n",
 894          $first, $last, $idx);
 895      $idx += $last - $first + 1;
 896        }
 897        $first=$u;
 898      }
 899      $last=$u;
 900    }
 901    printf ("  { .start = %#06x, .end = %#06x, .idx = %5d }, \n",
 902        $first, $last, $idx);
 903    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
 904 */
 905 const struct jisx0212_idx __jisx0212_from_ucs_idx[] =
 906 {
 907   { .start = 0x007e, .end = 0x007e, .idx =     0 },
 908   { .start = 0x00a1, .end = 0x00af, .idx =     1 },
 909   { .start = 0x00b8, .end = 0x017e, .idx =    16 },
 910   { .start = 0x01cd, .end = 0x01dc, .idx =   215 },
 911   { .start = 0x01f5, .end = 0x01f5, .idx =   231 },
 912   { .start = 0x02c7, .end = 0x02c7, .idx =   232 },
 913   { .start = 0x02d8, .end = 0x02dd, .idx =   233 },
 914   { .start = 0x0384, .end = 0x0390, .idx =   239 },
 915   { .start = 0x03aa, .end = 0x03b0, .idx =   252 },
 916   { .start = 0x03c2, .end = 0x03c2, .idx =   259 },
 917   { .start = 0x03ca, .end = 0x03ce, .idx =   260 },
 918   { .start = 0x0402, .end = 0x040f, .idx =   265 },
 919   { .start = 0x0452, .end = 0x045f, .idx =   279 },
 920   { .start = 0x2116, .end = 0x2116, .idx =   293 },
 921   { .start = 0x2122, .end = 0x2122, .idx =   294 },
 922   { .start = 0x4e02, .end = 0x4e05, .idx =   295 },
 923   { .start = 0x4e0c, .end = 0x4e12, .idx =   299 },
 924   { .start = 0x4e1f, .end = 0x4e35, .idx =   306 },
 925   { .start = 0x4e40, .end = 0x4e47, .idx =   329 },
 926   { .start = 0x4e51, .end = 0x4e51, .idx =   337 },
 927   { .start = 0x4e5a, .end = 0x4e5c, .idx =   338 },
 928   { .start = 0x4e63, .end = 0x4e69, .idx =   341 },
 929   { .start = 0x4e74, .end = 0x4e7f, .idx =   348 },
 930   { .start = 0x4e8d, .end = 0x4e8d, .idx =   360 },
 931   { .start = 0x4e96, .end = 0x4e9d, .idx =   361 },
 932   { .start = 0x4eaf, .end = 0x4eaf, .idx =   369 },
 933   { .start = 0x4eb9, .end = 0x4eb9, .idx =   370 },
 934   { .start = 0x4ec3, .end = 0x4ec3, .idx =   371 },
 935   { .start = 0x4ed0, .end = 0x4ed0, .idx =   372 },
 936   { .start = 0x4eda, .end = 0x4ee8, .idx =   373 },

1658 /* The values corresponding to the table can be computed using
1659 
1660     egrep '^0x[[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]][[:xdigit:]]' \
1661       .../eastasia/jis/jis0212.txt | awk '{ print $2, $1 }' |
1662     sort -u | perl tab.pl
1663 
1664    where tab.pl contains:
1665 
1666    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1667    $first=$last=$idx=0;
1668 
1669    sub fmt {
1670      printf ("\n ") if (($n % 6) == 0);
1671      ++$n;
1672      my($val) = pop(@_);
1673      printf (" \"\\x%02x\\x%02x\",",
1674          $val < 256 ? $val : int($val / 256),
1675          $val < 256 ? 0 : $val % 256);
1676    }
1677 
1678    while (<>) {
1679      local($ucs,$jis,%rest) = split;
1680      local($u)=hex($ucs);
1681      local($j)=hex($jis);
1682      if ($u - $last > 6) {
1683        if ($last != 0) {
1684      $idx += $last - $first + 1;
1685        }
1686        $first=$u;
1687      } else {
1688        for ($m = $last + 1; $m < $u; ++$m) {
1689      fmt (0);
1690        }
1691      }
1692      fmt ($j);
1693      $last=$u;
1694    }
1695    ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
1696 */
